20:49 might be ACTUAL tech. In videogames, they often do what's called a "ground check", meaning they check whether or not you are on a stable surface, in this case, to detect whether or not you are falling, but the defuser counts as ground and has its own collision, so because he and the defuser were falling together, the game registered him as touching the ground the entire time, negating all fall damage. This could probably be consistenly replicated, and maybe even come in handy during pro games.
Now that you have the Juan, Black Ice. We all expect a Juan Tap video for Christmas.
